1A- G 26706 - 36  (2017/11)
LOCAL AUTHORITIES ELECTION ORDINANCE (CHAPTER 262)
Division of Local Authority Areas into Polling Districts
Notice Under Section 12(1)
The Public is hereby notified that the Polling Districts of Local Authority Areas of Colombo Administrative District mentioned
in the Schedule here to that were valid for Parliamentary Elections have been amended for the purpose of Local Authorities
Elections as mentioned in the same.
W. M. C. K
UMUDUNEE WIJEKURUPPU,
Assistant Returning Officer,
Colombo District
(for returning Officer of Colombo District)
Colombo Metro Election Office,
Old Kotte Road,
Rajagiriya.
22nd November, 2017
The Gazette of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka
